#!/usr/bin/env python
# Author: Nike Dattani, nike@hpqc.org
'''
H2 in aug-cc-pV5Z
'''
import numpy as np
import pyscf
from pyscf.gto.basis import parse_gaussian
from pyscf import gto, scf, ao2mo, fci, ci

mol = pyscf.M(
    atom = 'H 0 0 0; H 0 0 1.4011',
    unit = 'bohr',
    basis = 'aug-cc-pv5z',
#   basis = {
#           'H' : parse_gaussian.load('/home/nike/AI_ENERGIES/H/av5z.gbs', 'H')
#   },
    charge = 0,
    spin = 0,
    verbose = 9,
    symmetry = True,
    symmetry_subgroup = 'Dooh',
    max_memory =20000,
)

#####################
## Hartree-Fock:
#####################
mf = mol.RHF().set(conv_tol=1e-10,max_cycle=999,direct_scf_tol=1e-14,chkfile = 'a5z.chk')
#mf.init_guess='atom'
#mf.init_guess='O_av7z_UHF.chk'
mf.kernel()

#####################
## post-Hartree-Fock:
#####################

#for sym in ['A1g','E1gx','E1gy','A1u','E1uy','E1ux']:
#for sym in ['A1g','E1gx','A1u','E1uy']:
#mci = ci.CISD(mf, mf.mo_coeff).set(conv_tol=1e-5,max_cycle=999,wfnsym = sym,nroots=2)
mci = ci.CISD(mf).set(conv_tol=1e-6,max_cycle=999,nroots=28)
e, civec = mci.kernel()
#e, civec = mci.kernel(ci0=np.load('civec.npy'))
np.save('civec.npy', civec)
print('{}: {}'.format(sym,e))

#####################
## END OF INPUT 
#####################
